          <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-jenkins-google-driver-uploader" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#jenkins-google-driver-uploader"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Jenkins Google Driver Uploader</h1>
<p dir="auto">This plugin allows you to upload artifacts to your google service account.</p>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-install" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#install"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Install</h1>
<p dir="auto">Create an HPI file to install in Jenkins (HPI file will be in
<code>target/google-drive-upload.hpi</code>).</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="mvn clean package"><pre><code>mvn clean package
</code></pre></div>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-screenshot" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#screenshot"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>ScreenShot</h1>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/general-mobile/jenkins-google-drive-uploader/blob/master/assets/jenkins-drive-uploader.png"><img src="/general-mobile/jenkins-google-drive-uploader/raw/master/assets/jenkins-drive-uploader.png" alt="sample_image" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-thanks" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#thanks"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Thanks</h1>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/mstipanov">Marko Stipanov</a> for creating <a href="https://github.com/mstipanov/google-drive-upload-plugin">Jenkins Google Driver Uploader</a>. This helps us a lot to create this plugin.</p>
</article>
        </div>
    </div>

        <div data-target="readme-toc.content" class="Box-body px-5 pb-5">
          <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-jenkins-google-driver-uploader" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#jenkins-google-driver-uploader"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Jenkins Google Driver Uploader</h1>
<p dir="auto">This plugin allows you to upload artifacts to your google service account.</p>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-install" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#install"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Install</h1>
<p dir="auto">Create an HPI file to install in Jenkins (HPI file will be in
<code>target/google-drive-upload.hpi</code>).</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="mvn clean package"><pre><code>mvn clean package
</code></pre></div>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-screenshot" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#screenshot"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>ScreenShot</h1>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/general-mobile/jenkins-google-drive-uploader/blob/master/assets/jenkins-drive-uploader.png"><img src="/general-mobile/jenkins-google-drive-uploader/raw/master/assets/jenkins-drive-uploader.png" alt="sample_image" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-thanks" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#thanks"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Thanks</h1>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/mstipanov">Marko Stipanov</a> for creating <a href="https://github.com/mstipanov/google-drive-upload-plugin">Jenkins Google Driver Uploader</a>. This helps us a lot to create this plugin.</p>

        <div data-target="readme-toc.content" class="Box-body px-5 pb-5">
          <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-jenkins-google-driver-uploader" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#jenkins-google-driver-uploader"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Jenkins Google Driver Uploader</h1>
<p dir="auto">This plugin allows you to upload artifacts to your google service account.</p>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-install" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#install"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Install</h1>
<p dir="auto">Create an HPI file to install in Jenkins (HPI file will be in
<code>target/google-drive-upload.hpi</code>).</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="mvn clean package"><pre><code>mvn clean package
</code></pre></div>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-screenshot" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#screenshot"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>ScreenShot</h1>
<p dir="auto"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/general-mobile/jenkins-google-drive-uploader/blob/master/assets/jenkins-drive-uploader.png"><img src="/general-mobile/jenkins-google-drive-uploader/raw/master/assets/jenkins-drive-uploader.png" alt="sample_image" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-thanks" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#thanks"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Thanks</h1>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/mstipanov">Marko Stipanov</a> for creating <a href="https://github.com/mstipanov/google-drive-upload-plugin">Jenkins Google Driver Uploader</a>. This helps us a lot to create this plugin.</p>
